The `restoreCustomOverrideRules` function is called when changing panel types (line 425 in PanelModel.ts shows it's in the `changeType` method context).\n\nSo the regression would occur when:\n1. A dashboard has a table panel with NO `fieldConfig.defaults.custom`\n2. But it has field overrides with `custom.displayMode`\n3. During migration to v38, the backend migration correctly migrates the overrides to `custom.cellOptions`\n4. But when the panel is loaded in the frontend, something goes wrong\n\nActually, let me reconsider. The `restoreCustomOverrideRules` function is about preserving custom properties when switching panel types. But the issue is about v38 migration where defaults.custom doesn't exist.\n\nLet me think about this differently. After the v38 migration, the overrides are correctly updated to use `custom.cellOptions`. But then during frontend processing, if some code assumes that `defaults.custom` exists and tries to access it, it could fail.\n\nActually, I think the real bug might be in the `cleanProperties` function at line 132:\n\n```typescript\n// If no child props found unset the main object\n\n\nif (!childPropFound) {\n  unset(obj, propName);\n}\n```\n\nWhen the `custom` object is empty (no child properties), it gets deleted entirely. This could cause overrides with custom properties to be dropped if the defaults don't have matching custom properties. The `filterFieldConfigOverrides` function at line 79-81 filters out overrides for properties that cannot be applied, which might be removing the custom overrides if the defaults structure doesn't support them.\n\nThe real issue is likely that `custom.cellOptions` isn't registered in the table plugin's field config registry, so the filtering logic removes those overrides as unrecognized The backend v38 migration correctly converts `custom.displayMode` → `custom.cellOptions` in overrides\n2. The frontend field config processing (`getPanelOptionsWithDefaults.ts`) filters out overrides based on registry lookups\n3. The conditional logic pathway assumes `defaults.custom` must exist to properly validate custom override properties\n4.
